<div class="text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-text mb-lg-sl56 mb-sl48 " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p><span class="body-small">Last updated: December 5, 2024 | Reviewed by <a data-title="liane-goulet" data-bs-target="#liane-goulet" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-class="sl-link sl-link-sm" class=" sl-link sl-link-sm" href="#">Liane Goulet</a></span></p>

</div>

    
</div>
<div class="text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-text mb-sm-sl40 mb-sl32 " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <h2>What is critical illness insurance?</h2>
<p>Critical illness insurance (CII) is coverage that can help Canadians or those living in Canada pay the additional costs associated with life-altering illnesses. It is a versatile solution that can address a variety of needs for many different people at different stages of life.</p>

</div>

    
</div>
<div class="text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-text mb-sm-sl40 mb-sl32 " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <h3>What can critical illness insurance cover?</h3>
<p>Illnesses commonly covered by CII include <a data-class="sl-link" class=" sl-link" href="#cancer" target="_self">cancer</a>, heart attack, stroke, major organ failure on waiting list, severe burns, and more.</p>
<p>Claims are assessed based on critical illnesses specifically covered in the clients critical illness insurance contract at time of issue. Covered illnesses must meet the specific definition requirements, and coverage is subject to exclusions and limitations.</p>

</div>

    
</div>
<div class="text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-text mb-lg-sl56 mb-sl48 " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <h3>Why is critical illness insurance important?</h3>
<p>If youre diagnosed with a covered illness, a CII policy can help you pay for expenses that your provincial or territorial health plan or other insurance doesnt cover, like home-care costs and more.</p>
<p>CII pays a lump-sum payment that you can use however you want; to help you, your family or business financially manage a life changing illness so that you can focus on your recovery.</p>

</div>

    
</div>
<div class="separator aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12">
  <hr class="mb-lg-sl56 mb-sl48 sl-divider hr " aria-hidden="true" data-sl-aem-component="separator">
</div>
<div class="text aem-GridColumn aem-GridColumn--default--12"><div class="cmp-text mb-sl24 " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <h2>Who is critical illness insurance for?</h2>
<p>CII is generally intended to help anyone manage financial hardship due to a covered critical illness.</p>

</div>

    
</div>

      <h3 class="h4 card-title">Complementary to health insurance</h3>
      <div class="card-text"><p>CII works alongside other types of coverage, like <a data-class="sl-link" class=" sl-link" href="/en/health/personal-health-insurance/" target="_self">Personal Health Insurance (PHI)</a> to cover additional expenses not paid for by regular medical plans.         <button data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" aria-label="Video transcript" class="accordion-button collapsed" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#accordionitem_1712751329089" aria-expanded="false" type="button">
          <span class="accordion-icon-container">
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-up fa-w-14 sl-icon hide" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-up" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M4.465 366.475l7.07 7.071c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0L224 178.053l195.494 195.493c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0l7.07-7.071c4.686-4.686 4.686-12.284 0-16.97l-211.05-211.051c-4.686-4.686-12.284-4.686-16.971 0L4.465 349.505c-4.687 4.686-4.687 12.284 0 16.97z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-up hide"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14 sl-icon show" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-down" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M443.5 162.6l-7.1-7.1c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0L224 351 28.5 155.5c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0l-7.1 7.1c-4.7 4.7-4.7 12.3 0 17l211 211.1c4.7 4.7 12.3 4.7 17 0l211-211.1c4.8-4.7 4.8-12.3.1-17z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-down show"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->

          <span class="accordion-item-heading h3">Video transcript</span>

      </h3>
      <div class="accordion-collapse collapse false" id="accordionitem_1712751329089">
        <div class="accordion-body" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel"><div class="text"><div class="cmp-text  " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p><span class="body-medium-bold">What is critical illness insurance?</span></p>
<p>Simply put, wed all like to imagine a future with perfect health. But the right time to plan for the unexpected is when you're healthy. Why? Because once you become ill, your options might be limited.</p>
<p>Critical illness insurance is designed to help you pay costs that may be associated with certain life-altering illnesses.</p>
<p>It provides additional funds if you become seriously ill. This way, you can focus on your health and not your finances.</p>
<p><span class="body-medium-bold">How does critical illness insurance work?</span></p>
<p>Lets say youre diagnosed with and survive one of the illnesses covered, as defined by your insurance policy. In such a case, you'll receive a one-time, lump-sum cash payment. You can then use that money any way you wish.</p>
<p><span class="body-medium-bold">Do you need critical illness insurance?</span></p>
<p>So ask yourself:</p>
<ul>
<li>Do your other insurance policies like life, group health, or disability plans offer enough coverage?</li>
<li>Would your retirement goals still be met if you had to take out, say, $50,000 for expenses related to a medical condition?</li>
<li>Can you afford to take on the costs associated with being seriously ill? This includes things like:<ul>
<li>loss of income,</li>
<li>travel to and from treatment, and</li>
<li>home-care costs.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p><span class="body-medium-bold">How can critical illness insurance help you?</span></p>
<p>It can help with those additional costs that come up.</p>
<p>Chances are you know someone who's been affected by serious health issues. Critical illness insurance will provide you with the peace of mind of knowing you're financially protected in case it happens to you. And, itll allow you to focus 100% on your own recovery.</p>
<p>For more tips and tools, visit sunlife.ca.</p>

</div>

    
</div>
</div>
      </div>
    </div>

          </span>
          <span class="accordion-item-heading h3">Do I need to take a medical exam for critical illness insurance?</span>
        </button>
      </h3>
      <div class="accordion-collapse false collapse" id="accordionitem_1732206332418" style="">
        <div class="accordion-body" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel"><div class="text"><div class="cmp-text  " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p>It depends on the product youre applying for. If youre applying online for <a data-class="sl-link" class=" sl-link" href="/en/health/critical-illness-insurance/express-critical-illness-insurance/" target="_self">Express Critical Illness Insurance</a>, then you wont have to answer any medical questions or undergo a medical exam.</p>
<p>However, if youre applying for <a data-class="sl-link" class=" sl-link" href="/en/health/critical-illness-insurance/sun-critical-illness-insurance/" target="_self">Sun Critical Illness Insurance</a>, which offers coverage up to $4,000,000, you may need to complete a medical exam during the application process.</p>

<div class="accordion-item " data-cmp-hook-accordion="item">
      <h3 class="h3 accordion-header" id="-id-1" data-single-expansion="true">
        <button data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" aria-label="Is a critical illness insurance payout taxable in Canada?" class="accordion-button collapsed" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#accordionitem_1732206349315" aria-expanded="false" type="button">
          <span class="accordion-icon-container">
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-up fa-w-14 sl-icon hide" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-up" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M4.465 366.475l7.07 7.071c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0L224 178.053l195.494 195.493c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0l7.07-7.071c4.686-4.686 4.686-12.284 0-16.97l-211.05-211.051c-4.686-4.686-12.284-4.686-16.971 0L4.465 349.505c-4.687 4.686-4.687 12.284 0 16.97z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-up hide"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14 sl-icon show" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-down" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M443.5 162.6l-7.1-7.1c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0L224 351 28.5 155.5c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0l-7.1 7.1c-4.7 4.7-4.7 12.3 0 17l211 211.1c4.7 4.7 12.3 4.7 17 0l211-211.1c4.8-4.7 4.8-12.3.1-17z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-down show"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
          </span>
          <span class="accordion-item-heading h3">Is a critical illness insurance payout taxable in Canada?</span>
        </button>
      </h3>
      <div class="accordion-collapse false collapse" id="accordionitem_1732206349315" style="">
        <div class="accordion-body" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel"><div class="text"><div class="cmp-text  " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p>In Canada, there are no specific tax laws governing CII policies. However, the Canada Revenue Agency (CRA) has developed its own position on the tax treatment of a benefit paid under a CII policy.</p>
<p>Based on the CRA's current position, Sun Life understands that&nbsp;<span class="body-medium-bold">benefits for individually owned CII policies are paid tax-free</span>.</p>
<p>Talk to a tax professional for more information.</p>

</div>

    
</div>
</div>
      </div>
    </div>
<div class="accordion-item " data-cmp-hook-accordion="item">
      <h3 class="h3 accordion-header" id="-id-2" data-single-expansion="true">
        <button data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" aria-label="How long is the waiting period for critical illness insurance?" class="accordion-button collapsed" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#accordionitem_1732206351420" aria-expanded="false" type="button">
          <span class="accordion-icon-container">
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-up fa-w-14 sl-icon hide" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-up" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M4.465 366.475l7.07 7.071c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0L224 178.053l195.494 195.493c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0l7.07-7.071c4.686-4.686 4.686-12.284 0-16.97l-211.05-211.051c-4.686-4.686-12.284-4.686-16.971 0L4.465 349.505c-4.687 4.686-4.687 12.284 0 16.97z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-up hide"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14 sl-icon show" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-down" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M443.5 162.6l-7.1-7.1c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0L224 351 28.5 155.5c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0l-7.1 7.1c-4.7 4.7-4.7 12.3 0 17l211 211.1c4.7 4.7 12.3 4.7 17 0l211-211.1c4.8-4.7 4.8-12.3.1-17z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-down show"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
          </span>
          <span class="accordion-item-heading h3">How long is the waiting period for critical illness insurance?</span>
        </button>
      </h3>
      <div class="accordion-collapse false collapse" id="accordionitem_1732206351420" style="">
        <div class="accordion-body" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel"><div class="text"><div class="cmp-text  " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p>The most common type of waiting period for CII is the survival period. In Canada, if included, the survival period is usually 30 days. This means that, in some cases, you are required to survive a minimum of 30 days after the diagnosis of the covered illness before you can submit a claim and receive the benefit.</p>
<p>Other covered illnesses or diseases, such as cancer, require your coverage to be in effect for a certain amount of time before youre eligible for the benefit.</p>
<p>For full details, please familiarize yourself with your policy or <a href="/en/find-an-advisor/" target="_self" class=" sl-link" data-class="sl-link">connect with an advisor</a>.</p>

</div>

    
</div>
</div>
      </div>
    </div>

        <button data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" aria-label="Does my child need critical illness insurance?" class="accordion-button collapsed" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#accordionitem_1732206360331" aria-expanded="false" type="button">

          </span>
          <span class="accordion-item-heading h3">Does my child need critical illness insurance?</span>
        </button>
      </h3>
      <div class="accordion-collapse false collapse" id="accordionitem_1732206360331" style="">
        <div class="accordion-body" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel"><div class="text"><div class="cmp-text  " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p>You may need critical illness insurance for a child if you think you cant afford all the expenses that may arise if your child is diagnosed with a covered critical illness.</p>
<p>For example, you may need to take time off work (resulting in income loss) to take care of your child. In such cases, a critical illness insurance plan for a child will give you a lump sum of money if your child ever gets one of the illnesses covered in the policy.</p>
<p><a href="/en/health/critical-illness-insurance/should-you-buy-critical-illness-insurance-for-your-child/" target="_self" class="sl-link-internal sl-link" data-class="sl-link" data-class-icon="sl-link-internal">Heres how to find out if your children need critical illness insurance<span class="visually-hidden">&nbsp;</span><svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-circle-right icn-hover-hidden" aria-hidden="false" title="opens an internal link" aria-labelledby="svg-inline--fa-title-b6absuBi8Xia" data-prefix="fak" data-icon="chevron-circle-right" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 492 512" data-fa-i2svg="" style="width: 0.9609375em;"><title id="svg-inline--fa-title-b6absuBi8Xia">opens an internal link</title><path fill="currentColor" d="M420.1 262.8a174.1 174.1 0 1 1 -348.2 0 174.1 174.1 0 1 1 348.2 0zM246 109.2a153.6 153.6 0 1 0 0 307.2 153.6 153.6 0 1 0 0-307.2zm-33.7 44L321.9 262.8 212.3 372.4l-14.5-14.5L293 262.8l-95.2-95.2 14.5-14.5z"></path></svg><!-- <i class="fak fa-chevron-circle-right icn-hover-hidden" aria-hidden="false" title="opens an internal link"></i> Font Awesome fontawesome.com --><svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-circle-right-hover icn-hover-show" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fak" data-icon="chevron-circle-right-hover" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 492 512" data-fa-i2svg="" style="width: 0.9609375em;"><path fill="currentColor" d="M246 88.7a174.1 174.1 0 1 0 0 348.2 174.1 174.1 0 1 0 0-348.2zm75.9 174.1L212.3 372.4l-14.5-14.5L293 262.8l-95.2-95.2 14.5-14.5L321.9 262.8z"></path></svg><!-- <i class="fak fa-chevron-circle-right-hover icn-hover-show" aria-hidden="true"></i> Font Awesome fontawesome.com --></a></p>

<div class="accordion-item " data-cmp-hook-accordion="item">
      <h3 class="h3 accordion-header" id="-id-6" data-single-expansion="true">
        <button data-cmp-hook-accordion="button" aria-label="What is the difference between life insurance and critical illness insurance?" class="accordion-button collapsed" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#accordionitem_1732206362739" aria-expanded="false" type="button">
          <span class="accordion-icon-container">
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-up fa-w-14 sl-icon hide" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-up" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M4.465 366.475l7.07 7.071c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0L224 178.053l195.494 195.493c4.686 4.686 12.284 4.686 16.971 0l7.07-7.071c4.686-4.686 4.686-12.284 0-16.97l-211.05-211.051c-4.686-4.686-12.284-4.686-16.971 0L4.465 349.505c-4.687 4.686-4.687 12.284 0 16.97z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-up hide"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
            <svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14 sl-icon show" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fal" data-icon="chevron-down" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" data-fa-i2svg=""><path fill="currentColor" d="M443.5 162.6l-7.1-7.1c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0L224 351 28.5 155.5c-4.7-4.7-12.3-4.7-17 0l-7.1 7.1c-4.7 4.7-4.7 12.3 0 17l211 211.1c4.7 4.7 12.3 4.7 17 0l211-211.1c4.8-4.7 4.8-12.3.1-17z"></path></svg><!-- <span class="sl-icon fal fa-chevron-down show"></span> Font Awesome fontawesome.com -->
          </span>
          <span class="accordion-item-heading h3">What is the difference between life insurance and critical illness insurance?</span>
        </button>
      </h3>
      <div class="accordion-collapse false collapse" id="accordionitem_1732206362739" style="">
        <div class="accordion-body" data-cmp-hook-accordion="panel"><div class="text"><div class="cmp-text  " data-sl-aem-component="text">
    <p>The main difference between critical illness insurance and life insurance is&nbsp;how&nbsp;the insurance benefit is triggered.</p>
<p>CII benefits are paid out when you or the insured person is coping with or recovering from a covered critical illness as defined in the contract.</p>
<p>Life insurance benefits, however, are paid out to your estate or named beneficiary when you die.</p>
<p><a href="/en/health/critical-illness-insurance/critical-illness-insurance-vs-life-insurance/" target="_self" class="sl-link-internal sl-link" data-class="sl-link" data-class-icon="sl-link-internal">Learn more about the difference between life insurance and critical illness insurance<span class="visually-hidden">&nbsp;</span><svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-circle-right icn-hover-hidden" aria-hidden="false" title="opens an internal link" aria-labelledby="svg-inline--fa-title-mky3Gn8lX0YG" data-prefix="fak" data-icon="chevron-circle-right" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 492 512" data-fa-i2svg="" style="width: 0.9609375em;"><title id="svg-inline--fa-title-mky3Gn8lX0YG">opens an internal link</title><path fill="currentColor" d="M420.1 262.8a174.1 174.1 0 1 1 -348.2 0 174.1 174.1 0 1 1 348.2 0zM246 109.2a153.6 153.6 0 1 0 0 307.2 153.6 153.6 0 1 0 0-307.2zm-33.7 44L321.9 262.8 212.3 372.4l-14.5-14.5L293 262.8l-95.2-95.2 14.5-14.5z"></path></svg><!-- <i class="fak fa-chevron-circle-right icn-hover-hidden" aria-hidden="false" title="opens an internal link"></i> Font Awesome fontawesome.com --><svg class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-circle-right-hover icn-hover-show" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fak" data-icon="chevron-circle-right-hover" role="img" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 492 512" data-fa-i2svg="" style="width: 0.9609375em;"><path fill="currentColor" d="M246 88.7a174.1 174.1 0 1 0 0 348.2 174.1 174.1 0 1 0 0-348.2zm75.9 174.1L212.3 372.4l-14.5-14.5L293 262.8l-95.2-95.2 14.5-14.5L321.9 262.8z"></path></svg><!-- <i class="fak fa-chevron-circle-right-hover icn-hover-show" aria-hidden="true"></i> Font Awesome fontawesome.com --></a></p>

</div>

    <div class="footer-content-container">
        <hr class="sl-divider hr" aria-hidden="true">
        <div class="footer-content">
            
            <div class="footer-body"><p><span class="h3">Lifes brighter under the sun</span></p>
<p><span class="footer-body">We acknowledge that Sun Life operates in many Territories and Treaties across Canada. Our Canadian headquarters in Waterloo are on the traditional territory of the Anishnaabeg, Haudenosaunee Confederacy and the Mississaugas of the Credit First Nations.</span></p>
<p><span class="footer-body">Today, Canada is still the home to many Indigenous, First Nations, Inuit, and Metis peoples from all across Turtle Island. We are grateful to have the opportunity to work in this territory. We offer this acknowledgment as a stepping stone towards honouring the original occupants, as a testimony to the oppression faced by Indigenous peoples, and our commitment to Indigenous communities and employees of Sun Life.</span><br>
</p>
<p><span class="footer-copy"> Sun Life Assurance Company of Canada. All rights reserved.</span></p>
</div>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            var coveoSearchlanguage = ""
            var searchConfig = {
                orgId: "sunlifefinancialincproductionapwbq5p7",
                token: "xx266e8be8-4de6-4bd4-9e58-5b7e2b8b986d",
                restUri: "https://sunlifefinancialincproductionapwbq5p7.org.coveo.com/rest/search",
                searchHub: "sunlifeCA",
                searchUrl: $('form[name="search-url"]').attr('action')
            };

            if ($('.advisorhub-sunlife-content-page').length > 0 || $('.advisorhub-sunlife-home-page').length > 0) {
                var advisorHubSegment = ContextHub.SegmentEngine.getResolvedSegments();
                var advisorHubManager = false;
                for (var i = 0; i < advisorHubSegment.length; i++) {
                    if (advisorHubSegment[i]["title"] == "Manager") {
                        advisorHubManager = true;
                        break;
                    }
                }

                var token = searchConfig.token.split('::');
                var searchHub = searchConfig.searchHub.split('::');
                console.log('advisor-hub Manager : ', advisorHubManager)
                if (advisorHubManager == true) {
                    searchConfig.token = token[0]
                    searchConfig.searchHub = searchHub[0]
                }
                else {
                    searchConfig.token = token[1]
                    searchConfig.searchHub = searchHub[1]
                }
            }

            //Configure a search endpoint.
            Coveo.SearchEndpoint.configureCloudV2Endpoint(searchConfig.orgId, searchConfig.token, searchConfig.restUri);

            let timeoutId;
            let tealiumRetryCount = 0;
            const TEALIUM_MAX_RETRIES = 20;
            function triggerCoveoAnalytics() {
                //Coveo UA
                const URLPrefix = "https://";
                const analyticsDomain = ".analytics.org.coveo.com";
                const analyticsURL = URLPrefix + searchConfig.orgId + analyticsDomain;
                coveoua("init", searchConfig.token, analyticsURL);
                coveoua("send", "view", {
                    contentIdKey: "url",
                    contentIdValue: utag_data.page_canonical_url,
                    contentType: utag_data.page_category
                });
                // Below code tracks analytics(coveo) for click on search results
                let CoveoAnalyticsEndpoint = analyticsURL+"/rest/ua";
                let $coveoAnalytics = $('div.CoveoAnalytics');
                $($coveoAnalytics).attr('data-endpoint', CoveoAnalyticsEndpoint);
            }

            function checkTealiumConsentAndRunAnalytics() {
                if (window.tealiumConsentRegister && Array.isArray(tealiumConsentRegister.currentDecision)) {
                    if (!tealiumConsentRegister.currentDecision.includes("C0002")) {
                        // Consent present, disable analytics
                        Coveo.disableAnalytics();
                    } else {
                        triggerCoveoAnalytics();
                    }
                    if(timeoutId) {
                        clearTimeout(timeoutId); // Clear the timeout if it was set
                    }
                } else if (tealiumRetryCount < TEALIUM_MAX_RETRIES) {
                    tealiumRetryCount++;
                    timeoutId = setTimeout(checkTealiumConsentAndRunAnalytics, 100);
                } else {
                    // After max retries, fallback to analytics
                    triggerCoveoAnalytics();
                    if(timeoutId) {
                        clearTimeout(timeoutId);
                    }
                }
            }
            checkTealiumConsentAndRunAnalytics();
        </script>
